# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/moderation.js

1| // moderation.js - Gestion des bans et warns
2| 
3| // Vérifier si un utilisateur est banni
4| async function isBanned(pool, pseudo, ip, fingerprint) {
5|     // 1. Vérifier par pseudo
6|     const result = await pool.query(
7|         `SELECT * FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1 AND is_banned = true`,
8|         [pseudo]
9|     );
10|     if (result.rows.length > 0) return true;
11| 
12|     // 2. Plus tard : vérifier par IP + fingerprint
13|     return false;
14| }
15| 
16| // Appliquer le ban : déconnecter immédiatement
17| function disconnectBannedUser(io, users, pseudo, reason) {
18|     // Parcourir l'objet users avec Object.entries()
19|     for (let [socketId, userData] of Object.entries(users)) {
20|         if (userData.pseudo === pseudo) {
21|             io.to(socketId).emit('force logout', { reason: `Vous avez été banni : ${reason}` });
22|             const socket = io.sockets.sockets.get(socketId);
23|             if (socket) socket.disconnect();
24|             delete users[socketId];
25|             break;
26|         }
27|     }
28| }
29| 
30| 
31| 
32| module.exports = { isBanned, disconnectBannedUser };

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/generate-icons.js

1| const fs = require('fs');
2| const { createCanvas } = require('canvas');
3| 
4| // Tailles requises pour la PWA
5| const sizes = [72, 96, 128, 144, 152, 192, 384, 512];
6| 
7| // Couleurs
8| const bgColor = '#667eea';
9| const envelopeColor = '#ffffff';
10| const flapColor = '#ffffff';
11| 
12| // Créer le dossier icons s'il n'existe pas
13| if (!fs.existsSync('./public/icons')) {
14|     fs.mkdirSync('./public/icons', { recursive: true });
15| }
16| 
17| sizes.forEach(size => {
18|     const canvas = createCanvas(size, size);
19|     const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
20| 
21|     // Fond
22|     ctx.fillStyle = bgColor;
23|     ctx.fillRect(0, 0, size, size);
24| 
25|     // Dessiner l'enveloppe
26|     const padding = size * 0.15;
27|     const w = size - (padding * 2);
28|     const h = w * 0.7;
29|     const x = padding;
30|     const y = (size - h) / 2;
31| 
32|     ctx.fillStyle = envelopeColor;
33|     ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
34| 
35|     // Rabat de l'enveloppe (triangle)
36|     ctx.beginPath();
37|     ctx.moveTo(x, y);
38|     ctx.lineTo(x + w / 2, y + h / 2);
39|     ctx.lineTo(x + w, y);
40|     ctx.fillStyle = flapColor;
41|     ctx.fill();
42| 
43|     // Contour
44|     ctx.strokeStyle = bgColor;
45|     ctx.lineWidth = size * 0.02;
46|     ctx.strokeRect(x, y, w, h);
47| 
48|     // Cercle du sceau (optionnel)
49|     ctx.beginPath();
50|     ctx.arc(x + w / 2, y + h / 2, w * 0.12, 0, 2 * Math.PI);
51|     ctx.fillStyle = bgColor;
52|     ctx.fill();
53| 
54|     // Sauvegarder
55|     const buffer = canvas.toBuffer('image/png');
56|     fs.writeFileSync(`./public/icons/icon-${size}.png`, buffer);
57|     console.log(`✅ Généré : icon-${size}.png`);
58| });
59| 
60| console.log('🎉 Toutes les icônes ont été générées !');

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/modules/socket-handlers.js

1| ﻿// modules/socket-handlers.js
2| module.exports = function (io, pool, users, disconnectionTimers, updateActivity, REPORTS_THRESHOLD, REPORTS_WINDOW_MINUTES, TEMP_BAN_MINUTES) {
3|     io.on('connection', (socket) => {
4|         console.log('🔌 Nouvelle connexion :', socket.id);
5| 
6|         socket.on('user join', async (userInfo) => {
7|             if (!userInfo || !userInfo.pseudo) {
8|                 socket.emit('join error', { error: 'Pseudo requis pour rejoindre' });
9|                 return;
10| 
11|             }
12| 
13|             // Récupérer l'IP du client
14|             const clientIp = socket.handshake.headers['x-forwarded-for']
15|                 ? socket.handshake.headers['x-forwarded-for'].split(',')[0]
16|                 : socket.conn.remoteAddress;
17| 
18|             console.log(`📡 Connexion de ${userInfo.pseudo} depuis IP: ${clientIp}`);
19| 
20| 
21|             // ♻️ ANNUULATION DU MINUTEUR DE SUPPRESSION (Cas du F5)
22|             if (disconnectionTimers[userInfo.pseudo]) {
23|                 clearTimeout(disconnectionTimers[userInfo.pseudo]);
24|                 delete disconnectionTimers[userInfo.pseudo];
25|                 console.log(`♻️ Reconnexion rapide (F5) détectée pour ${userInfo.pseudo}. Session préservée.`);
26|             }
27| 
28|             // Récupérer la date de création depuis la base
29|             let firstConnectedAt = Date.now();
30|             try {
31|                 const result = await pool.query(
32|                     `SELECT first_connected_at FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1`,
33|                     [userInfo.pseudo]
34|                 );
35|                 if (result.rows.length > 0 && result.rows[0].first_connected_at) {
36|                     firstConnectedAt = new Date(result.rows[0].first_connected_at).getTime();
37|                 } else {
38|                     // Si first_connected_at est NULL, on le met à jour avec l’heure actuelle
39|                     await pool.query(
40|                         `UPDATE users SET first_connected_at = NOW() WHERE pseudo = $1`,
41|                         [userInfo.pseudo]
42|                     );
43|                 }
44|             } catch (err) {
45|                 console.error('Erreur récupération first_connected_at:', err.message);
46|             }
47| 
48|             // Nettoyer les anciennes sockets du même pseudo
49|             Object.keys(users).forEach((id) => {
50|                 if (users[id].pseudo === userInfo.pseudo) {
51|                     console.log(`🧹 Suppression de l'ancienne socket ${id} de ${userInfo.pseudo}`);
52|                     delete users[id];
53|                 }
54|             });
55| 
56| 
57|             users[socket.id] = {
58|                 ...userInfo,
59|                 socketId: socket.id,
60|                 firstConnectedAt: firstConnectedAt,
61|                 ip: clientIp  // ← Ajoute l'IP
62|             };
63|             console.log(`✅ ${userInfo.pseudo} a rejoint (${socket.id})`);
64|             updateActivity(socket.id);
65| 
66|             // Stocker le fingerprint et l'IP dans la base
67|             if (userInfo.fingerprint) {
68|                 try {
69|                     // Vérifier si le fingerprint existe déjà
70|                     const existingFp = await pool.query(
71|                         'SELECT id FROM fingerprints WHERE fingerprint_hash = $1',
72|                         [userInfo.fingerprint]
73|                     );
74| 
75|                     let fingerprintId;
76|                     if (existingFp.rows.length > 0) {
77|                         fingerprintId = existingFp.rows[0].id;
78|                         // Mettre à jour last_seen et notes
79|                         await pool.query(
80|                             `UPDATE fingerprints 
81|                              SET last_seen = NOW(), 
82|                                  notes = CASE 
83|                                      WHEN notes IS NULL THEN $1
84|                                      ELSE notes || ' | ' || $1
85|                                  END
86|                              WHERE id = $2`,
87|                             [`IP: ${clientIp}`, fingerprintId]
88|                         );
89|                     } else {
90|                         // Créer un nouveau fingerprint
91|                         const newFp = await pool.query(
92|                             `INSERT INTO fingerprints (fingerprint_hash, first_seen, last_seen, notes) 
93|                              VALUES ($1, NOW(), NOW(), $2)
94|                              RETURNING id`,
95|                             [userInfo.fingerprint, `IP: ${clientIp}`]
96|                         );
97|                         fingerprintId = newFp.rows[0].id;
98|                     }
99| 
100|                     // Lier le fingerprint à l'utilisateur
101|                     await pool.query(
102|                         'UPDATE users SET fingerprint_id = $1, last_ip = $2 WHERE pseudo = $3',
103|                         [fingerprintId, clientIp, userInfo.pseudo]
104|                     );
105| 
106| 
107|                     console.log(`🔒 Fingerprint lié pour ${userInfo.pseudo} (ID: ${fingerprintId})`);
108|                 } catch (err) {
109|                     console.error('Erreur stockage fingerprint/IP:', err);
110|                 }
111|             } else {
112|                 console.warn(`⚠️ Pas de fingerprint pour ${userInfo.pseudo}`);
113|             }
114| 
115|             // Tri par date de première connexion (plus ancien en bas, plus récent en haut)
116|             const usersList = Object.values(users).sort((a, b) => (b.firstConnectedAt || 0) - (a.firstConnectedAt || 0)).map(u => ({
117|                 pseudo: u.pseudo,
118|                 age: u.age,
119|                 tendencies: u.tendencies,
120|                 gender: u.gender,
121|                 purpose: u.purpose,
122|                 bio: u.bio,
123|                 locationCode: u.locationCode,
124|                 locationName: u.locationName,
125|                 socketId: u.socketId
126|             }));
127|             io.emit('update users', usersList);
128|             socket.emit('join confirmed', { success: true, user: userInfo });
129|         });
130| 
131| 
132|         // Heartbeat pour mettre à jour lastSeen
133|         socket.on('heartbeat', () => {
134|             if (users[socket.id]) {
135|                 users[socket.id].lastSeen = Date.now();
136|             }
137|         });
138| 
139| 
140|         socket.on('private message', (data) => {
141|             const { toSocketId, message, fromPseudo } = data;
142|             console.log(`💬 Message privé de ${fromPseudo} vers ${toSocketId}: ${message}`);
143|             updateActivity(socket.id);
144|             socket.to(toSocketId).emit('private message received', {
145|                 message: message,
146|                 fromPseudo: fromPseudo,
147|                 fromSocketId: socket.id
148|             });
149|             socket.emit('message sent confirmation', { message: message, to: toSocketId });
150|         });
151| 
152|         // Gestion des signalements utilisateur
153|         socket.on('report user', async (data) => {
154|             const { targetPseudo } = data;
155| 
156|             // Récupérer le pseudo du signaleur depuis users[socket.id]
157|             const reporterPseudo = users[socket.id]?.pseudo;
158|             if (!reporterPseudo) {
159|                 socket.emit('report_error', { error: 'Utilisateur non identifié' });
160|                 return;
161|             }
162| 
163|             if (!targetPseudo || targetPseudo === reporterPseudo) {
164|                 socket.emit('report_error', { error: 'Signalement invalide' });
165|                 return;
166|             }
167| 
168|             try {
169|                 // 1. Insérer le signalement
170|                 await pool.query(
171|                     'INSERT INTO reports (reporter_pseudo, target_pseudo) VALUES ($1, $2)',
172|                     [reporterPseudo, targetPseudo]
173|                 );
174| 
175|                 // 2. Utiliser les constantes de server.js
176|                 const threshold = REPORTS_THRESHOLD;
177| 
178|                 // 3. Récupérer la date de fin du dernier ban (si existe)
179|                 const lastBan = await pool.query(
180|                     `SELECT expires_at FROM temp_bans 
181|                     WHERE user_pseudo = $1 
182|                     ORDER BY expires_at DESC LIMIT 1`,
183|                     [targetPseudo]
184|                 );
185| 
186|                 let sinceDate = `NOW() - INTERVAL '${REPORTS_WINDOW_MINUTES} minutes'`;
187|                 if (lastBan.rows.length > 0) {
188|                     const lastBanExpiry = lastBan.rows[0].expires_at;
189|                     // Prendre la date la plus récente entre la fin du dernier ban et la fenêtre
190|                     sinceDate = `GREATEST(NOW() - INTERVAL '${REPORTS_WINDOW_MINUTES} minutes', '${lastBanExpiry.toISOString()}')`;
191|                 }
192| 
193|                 const countRes = await pool.query(
194|                     `SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT reporter_pseudo) FROM reports 
195|                     WHERE target_pseudo = $1 
196|                     AND created_at > ${sinceDate}`,
197|                     [targetPseudo]
198|                 );
199|                 const reportCount = parseInt(countRes.rows[0].count);
200| 
201|                 // 4. Confirmation au signaleur
202|                 socket.emit('report_confirmation', {
203|                     targetPseudo,
204|                     reportCount,
205|                     threshold,
206|                     willTrigger: reportCount >= threshold
207|                 });
208| 
209|                 // 5. Si seuil atteint, déclencher temp_ban (10 minutes)
210|                 if (reportCount >= threshold) {
211|                     const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + TEMP_BAN_MINUTES * 60 * 1000);
212| 
213|                     await pool.query(
214|                         `INSERT INTO temp_bans (user_pseudo, expires_at, reason) 
215|                          VALUES ($1, $2, $3)
216|                          ON CONFLICT (user_pseudo) DO UPDATE 
217|                          SET expires_at = EXCLUDED.expires_at, reason = EXCLUDED.reason`,
218|                         [targetPseudo, expiresAt, `${reportCount} signalements reçus`]
219|                     );
220| 
221|                     // Journaliser l'action
222|                     await pool.query(
223|                         `INSERT INTO moderation_actions (admin_pseudo, action_type, target_pseudo, duration_minutes, reason)
224|                          VALUES ('SYSTEM', 'temp_ban', $1, 10, $2)`,
225|                         [targetPseudo, `Ban auto après ${reportCount} signalements`]
226|                     );
227| 
228|                     // Déconnecter l'utilisateur cible s'il est connecté
229|                     const targetSocketEntry = Object.entries(users).find(([id, u]) => u.pseudo === targetPseudo);
230|                     if (targetSocketEntry) {
231|                         const targetSocketId = targetSocketEntry[0];
232|                         io.to(targetSocketId).emit('force logout', {
233|                             reason: `Vous avez été banni temporairement (10 minutes) pour comportement abusif.`
234|                         });
235|                     }
236| 
237|                     // Notifier tous les admins connectés (optionnel)
238|                     io.emit('new_report_auto_ban', {
239|                         targetPseudo,
240|                         reportCount,
241|                         duration: 10
242|                     });
243| 
244|                     console.log(`🔨 Auto-ban: ${targetPseudo} banni 10 min (${reportCount} signalements)`);
245|                 }
246|             } catch (err) {
247|                 console.error('Erreur lors du signalement:', err);
248|                 socket.emit('report_error', { error: 'Erreur serveur' });
249|             }
250|         });
251| 
252|         socket.on('disconnect', () => {
253|             console.log("🔥 DISCONNECT DÉCLENCHÉ pour socket:", socket.id);
254|             console.log(`🔌 DISCONNECT: Suppression de ${users[socket.id]?.pseudo} (socket: ${socket.id})`);
255|             const userInfo = users[socket.id];
256|             if (userInfo && userInfo.pseudo) {
257|                 const pseudo = userInfo.pseudo;
258|                 console.log(`🔌 Déconnexion immédiate de ${pseudo}`);
259| 
260|                 delete users[socket.id];
261|                 console.log(`🗑️ users après suppression:`, Object.keys(users).length, "connectés");
262| 
263| 
264|                 const usersList = Object.values(users).map(u => ({
265|                     pseudo: u.pseudo,
266|                     age: u.age,
267|                     tendencies: u.tendencies,
268|                     gender: u.gender,
269|                     purpose: u.purpose,
270|                     bio: u.bio,
271|                     locationCode: u.locationCode,
272|                     locationName: u.locationName,
273|                     socketId: u.socketId
274|                 }));
275|                 io.emit('update users', usersList);
276|             }
277| 
278|         });
279| 
280|     });
281| 
282| };

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/modules/cleanup.js

1| // options.js - Tâches annexes (nettoyage, surveillance inactivité)
2| const { Pool } = require('pg');
3| // 1. NETTOYAGE PÉRIODIQUE DES VISITEURS DÉCONNECTÉS
4| function startCleanup(pool, getOnlineUsers, intervalMs = 60 * 1000) {
5|     console.log(`🧹 Nettoyage programmé toutes les ${intervalMs / 1000} secondes`);
6|     setInterval(async () => {
7|         try {
8|             const onlinePseudos = getOnlineUsers();
9|             if (onlinePseudos.length > 0) {
10|                 const placeholders = onlinePseudos.map((_, i) => `$${i + 1}`).join(',');
11|                 const result = await pool.query(
12|                     `DELETE FROM users WHERE pseudo NOT IN (${placeholders}) AND (is_member = false OR is_member IS NULL)`,
13|                     onlinePseudos
14|                 );
15|                 if (result.rowCount > 0) console.log(`🧹 ${result.rowCount} visiteur(s) supprimé(s)`);
16|             } else {
17|                 const result = await pool.query("DELETE FROM users WHERE is_member = false OR is_member IS NULL");
18|                 if (result.rowCount > 0) console.log(`🧹 Nettoyage complet: ${result.rowCount} visiteur(s) supprimé(s)`);
19|             }
20|         } catch (err) {
21|             console.error('❌ Erreur nettoyage:', err.message);
22|         }
23|     }, intervalMs);
24| }
25| 
26| // 2. SURVEILLANCE D’INACTIVITÉ
27| function startInactivityWatch(io, users, pool, inactivityMinutes = 5, checkIntervalMs = 60 * 1000) {
28|     console.log(`⏱️ Surveillance inactivité : déconnexion après ${inactivityMinutes} minutes sans activité`);
29| 
30|     const lastActivity = new Map();
31| 
32|     function updateActivity(socketId) {
33|         lastActivity.set(socketId, Date.now());
34|     }
35| 
36|     setInterval(async () => {
37|         const now = Date.now();
38|         const timeoutMs = inactivityMinutes * 60 * 1000;
39| 
40|         for (const [socketId, user] of Object.entries(users)) {
41|             const last = lastActivity.get(socketId);
42|             if (last && (now - last) > timeoutMs) {
43|                 console.log(`⏰ ${user.pseudo} déconnecté pour inactivité (${inactivityMinutes} min)`);
44| 
45|                 const socket = io.sockets.sockets.get(socketId);
46|                 if (socket) {
47|                     socket.emit('force logout', {
48|                         reason: `Inactivité prolongée (${inactivityMinutes} minutes sans activité). Vous avez été déconnecté.`
49|                     });
50|                     socket.disconnect(true);
51|                 }
52| 
53|                 try {
54|                     await pool.query('DELETE FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1', [user.pseudo]);
55|                     console.log(`🗑️ ${user.pseudo} supprimé de la base pour inactivité`);
56|                 } catch (err) {
57|                     console.error('Erreur suppression inactif:', err.message);
58|                 }
59| 
60|                 delete users[socketId];
61|                 lastActivity.delete(socketId);
62| 
63|                 const usersList = Object.values(users).sort((a, b) => (b.firstConnectedAt || 0) - (a.firstConnectedAt || 0)).map(u => ({
64|                     pseudo: u.pseudo,
65|                     age: u.age,
66|                     tendencies: u.tendencies,
67|                     gender: u.gender,
68|                     purpose: u.purpose,
69|                     bio: u.bio,
70|                     locationCode: u.locationCode,
71|                     locationName: u.locationName,
72|                     socketId: u.socketId
73|                 }));
74|                 io.emit('update users', usersList);
75|             }
76|         }
77|     }, checkIntervalMs);
78| 
79|     return { updateActivity };
80| }
81| 
82| // ========== NETTOYAGE AUTO DU JOURNAL ET SIGNALEMENTS ==========
83| async function cleanOldData(pool, LOGS_RETENTION_DAYS, REPORTS_RETENTION_DAYS) {
84|     try {
85|         // Nettoyer le journal (moderation_actions)
86|         const logsResult = await pool.query(
87|             `DELETE FROM moderation_actions 
88|              WHERE created_at < NOW() - INTERVAL '${LOGS_RETENTION_DAYS} days'`
89|         );
90|         if (logsResult.rowCount > 0) {
91|             console.log(`🧹 Nettoyage auto journal: ${logsResult.rowCount} entrées supprimées (> ${LOGS_RETENTION_DAYS} jours)`);
92|         }
93| 
94|         // Nettoyer les signalements (reports)
95|         const reportsResult = await pool.query(
96|             `DELETE FROM reports 
97|              WHERE created_at < NOW() - INTERVAL '${REPORTS_RETENTION_DAYS} days'`
98|         );
99|         if (reportsResult.rowCount > 0) {
100|             console.log(`🧹 Nettoyage auto signalements: ${reportsResult.rowCount} signalements supprimés (> ${REPORTS_RETENTION_DAYS} jours)`);
101|         }
102|     } catch (err) {
103|         console.error('❌ Erreur nettoyage auto:', err);
104|     }
105| }
106| 
107| module.exports = { startCleanup, startInactivityWatch, cleanOldData };

2| const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');

5| module.exports = function (app, pool, io, users) {
6|     // ========== ROUTES ADMIN ==========
7|     app.post('/api/admin/login', async (req, res) => {
8|         const { username, password } = req.body;
9| 
10|         try {
11|             const result = await pool.query(
12|                 `SELECT id, username, password_hash, is_active FROM admins WHERE username = $1`,
13|                 [username]
14|             );
15| 
16|             if (result.rows.length === 0) {
17|                 return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Identifiants incorrects' });
18|             }
19| 
20|             const admin = result.rows[0];
21| 
22|             if (!admin.is_active) {
23|                 return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Compte désactivé' });
24|             }
25| 
26|             const isValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, admin.password_hash);
27| 
28|             if (!isValid) {
29|                 return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Identifiants incorrects' });
30|             }
31| 
32|             // CRÉER LA SESSION
33|             req.session.adminId = admin.id;
34|             req.session.isAdmin = true;
35|             req.session.adminUsername = admin.username;
36| 
37|             // FORCER L'INSERTION DANS admin_sessions
38|             try {
39|                 const sessionId = req.session.id;
40|                 console.log('📝 Tentative insertion - Session ID:', sessionId);
41|                 console.log('📝 Tentative insertion - Admin ID:', admin.id);
42| 
43|                 const insertResult = await pool.query(
44|                     `INSERT INTO admin_sessions (session_id, admin_id, is_logged_in, login_time, last_activity) 
45|                  VALUES ($1, $2, true, NOW(), NOW())
46|                  ON CONFLICT (session_id) DO UPDATE 
47|                  SET is_logged_in = true, last_activity = NOW()
48|                  RETURNING *`,
49|                     [sessionId, admin.id]
50|                 );
51| 
52|                 console.log('✅ SUCCÈS - Ligne insérée:', insertResult.rows[0]);
53|             } catch (dbErr) {
54|                 console.error('❌ ÉCHEC INSERTION:', dbErr.message);
55|                 console.error('Détails:', dbErr);
56|             }
57| 
58|             res.json({ success: true, admin: { id: admin.id, username: admin.username } });
59| 
60|         } catch (err) {
61|             console.error('Erreur login admin:', err);
62|             res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: 'Erreur serveur' });
63|         }
64|     });

77|             }
78|         }
79|

81|             if (err) {
82|                 return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erreur déconnexion' });
83|             }

85|         });

92|         }

110|                 'UPDATE users SET warnings = COALESCE(warnings, 0) + 1 WHERE pseudo = $1 RETURNING warnings',
111|                 [pseudo]

113|

141|

152|             disconnectBannedUser(io, users, pseudo, reason);

193|                  VALUES ($1, true, $2, NOW())`,
194|                     [fingerprint, reason || 'Banni par admin']
195|                 );
196|             } else {
197|                 await pool.query(
198|                     `UPDATE fingerprints SET is_banned = true, ban_reason = $1, banned_at = NOW() 
199|                  WHERE fingerprint_hash = $2`,
200|                     [reason || 'Banni par admin', fingerprint]
201|                 );
202|             }
203|             const usersToKick = await pool.query(
204|                 `SELECT u.pseudo FROM users u
205|              JOIN fingerprints f ON u.fingerprint_id = f.id
206|              WHERE f.fingerprint_hash = $1`,
207|                 [fingerprint]
208|             );
209|             for (const user of usersToKick.rows) {
210|                 disconnectBannedUser(io, users, user.pseudo, reason || 'Banni par admin');
211|             }
212|             res.json({ success: true, message: `Empreinte bannie, ${usersToKick.rowCount} utilisateur(s) déconnecté(s)` });
213|         } catch (err) {
214|             console.error('Erreur ban fingerprint:', err);
215|             res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erreur serveur' });
216|         }
217|     });
218| 
219|     // GET /api/admin/reports - Liste des signalements

225|             SELECT r.*, 
226|                    u1.pseudo as reporter_exists,
227|                    u2.pseudo as target_exists
228|             FROM reports r

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/modules/routes/api-auth.js

1| ﻿// modules/routes/api-auth.js
2| const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
3| const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'meetgay_super_secret_key_2026';
4| 
5| module.exports = function (app, pool) {
6|     // ========== CHECK TOKEN ==========
7|     app.get('/api/check-token', (req, res) => {
8|         const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(' ')[1];
9|         if (!token) return res.status(401).json({ valid: false });
10| 
11|         try {
12|             const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
13|             res.status(200).json({ valid: true, pseudo: decoded.pseudo });
14|         } catch (err) {
15|             res.status(401).json({ valid: false });
16|         }
17|     });
18| 
19|     // ========== REGISTER ==========
20|     app.post('/api/register', async (req, res) => {
21|         try {
22|             console.log("🔵 1. Début register, body reçu:", req.body);
23|             const { pseudo, age, tendencies, locationCode, locationName, bio, gender, purpose, fingerprint } = req.body;
24| 
25|             if (!pseudo || !age) {
26|                 return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Pseudo et âge requis' });
27|             }
28|             if (!fingerprint) {
29|                 return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Empreinte numérique requise' });
30|             }
31| 
32|             const banCheck = await pool.query(
33|                 `SELECT is_banned, ban_reason FROM fingerprints WHERE fingerprint_hash = $1`,
34|                 [fingerprint]
35|             );
36|             if (banCheck.rows.length > 0 && banCheck.rows[0].is_banned) {
37|                 return res.status(403).json({
38|                     error: 'Accès refusé',
39|                     reason: banCheck.rows[0].ban_reason || 'Votre empreinte est bannie'
40|                 });
41|             }
42| 
43|             const fingerprintResult = await pool.query(
44|                 `INSERT INTO fingerprints (fingerprint_hash, last_seen) 
45|                  VALUES ($1, NOW()) 
46|                  ON CONFLICT (fingerprint_hash) 
47|                  DO UPDATE SET last_seen = NOW()
48|                  RETURNING id`,
49|                 [fingerprint]
50|             );
51|             const fingerprintId = fingerprintResult.rows[0].id;
52| 
53|             const existingUser = await pool.query('SELECT id FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1', [pseudo]);
54|             if (existingUser.rows.length > 0) {
55|                 await pool.query('UPDATE users SET token_version = token_version + 1 WHERE pseudo = $1', [pseudo]);
56|             }
57| 
58|             const result = await pool.query(
59|                 `INSERT INTO users (pseudo, age, tendencies, location_code, location_name, bio, gender, purpose, fingerprint_id)
60|                  VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9)
61|                  ON CONFLICT (pseudo) DO NOTHING
62|                  RETURNING *`,
63|                 [pseudo, age, tendencies, locationCode, locationName, bio, gender, purpose, fingerprintId]
64|             );
65| 
66|             if (result.rows.length === 0) {
67|                 return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Pseudo déjà utilisé' });
68|             }
69| 
70|             res.json({ success: true, user: result.rows[0] });
71|         } catch (err) {
72|             console.error("Erreur inscription:", err);
73|             res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erreur serveur' });
74|         }
75|     });
76| 
77|     // ========== LOGIN ==========
78|     app.post('/api/login', async (req, res) => {
79|         const { pseudo } = req.body;
80|         if (!pseudo) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Pseudo requis' });
81|         try {
82|             const result = await pool.query('SELECT * FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1', [pseudo]);
83|             if (result.rows.length === 0) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Utilisateur non trouvé' });
84|             const user = result.rows[0];
85| 
86|             // Vérifier si le fingerprint est banni
87|             if (user.fingerprint_id) {
88|                 const bannedCheck = await pool.query(
89|                     `SELECT is_banned, ban_reason, banned_at FROM fingerprints 
90|          WHERE id = $1 AND is_banned = true`,
91|                     [user.fingerprint_id]
92|                 );
93| 
94|                 if (bannedCheck.rows.length > 0) {
95|                     const ban = bannedCheck.rows[0];
96|                     return res.status(403).json({
97|                         success: false,
98|                         error: 'fingerprint_banned',
99|                         message: `⛔ Votre navigateur est banni depuis le ${new Date(ban.banned_at).toLocaleString()}. Raison: ${ban.ban_reason || 'Comportement abusif'}`
100|                     });
101|                 }
102|             }
103| 
104|             // Vérifier si l'IP est bannie (optionnel)
105|             const ip = req.headers['x-forwarded-for']?.split(',')[0] || req.socket.remoteAddress;
106|             const ipBanned = await pool.query(
107|                 `SELECT is_banned FROM ip_bans WHERE ip_address = $1 AND is_banned = true`,
108|                 [ip]
109|             );
110|             if (ipBanned.rows.length > 0) {
111|                 return res.status(403).json({
112|                     success: false,
113|                     error: 'ip_banned',
114|                     message: '⛔ Votre adresse IP est bannie.'
115|                 });
116|             }
117| 
118|             // 🔍 VÉRIFICATION BAN TEMPORAIRE
119|             const banCheck = await pool.query(
120|                 `SELECT expires_at FROM temp_bans 
121|                  WHERE user_pseudo = $1 AND expires_at > NOW()`,
122|                 [pseudo]
123|             );
124| 
125|             if (banCheck.rows.length > 0) {
126|                 const expiresAt = banCheck.rows[0].expires_at;
127|                 const dateStr = new Date(expiresAt).toLocaleString();
128|                 return res.status(403).json({
129|                     error: 'banni_temporaire',
130|                     message: `⛔ Vous êtes banni jusqu'au ${dateStr} pour comportement abusif.`
131|                 });
132|             }
133|             // FIN VÉRIFICATION BAN
134| 
135|             const token = jwt.sign({ id: user.id, pseudo: user.pseudo, role: user.role || 'user' }, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '24h' });
136|             res.json({ success: true, token, user: { pseudo: user.pseudo, role: user.role } });
137|         } catch (err) {
138|             console.error('Erreur login:', err);
139|             res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erreur serveur' });
140|         }
141|     });
142| 
143|     // ========== DELETE USER ==========
144|     app.post('/api/delete-user', async (req, res) => {
145|         let pseudo = req.body.pseudo;
146| 
147|         if (!pseudo && req.body) {
148|             try {
149|                 if (typeof req.body === 'object') pseudo = req.body.pseudo;
150|                 else if (typeof req.body === 'string') {
151|                     const parsed = JSON.parse(req.body);
152|                     pseudo = parsed.pseudo;
153|                 }
154|             } catch (e) {
155|                 // Ignoré silencieusement
156|             }
157|         }
158| 
159|         if (!pseudo) {
160|             console.log(`🚪 Fermeture de page sans pseudo détecté (déjà géré par Socket.IO)`);
161|             return res.json({ success: true, message: 'Déconnexion propre' });
162|         }
163| 
164|         try {
165|             const result = await pool.query('DELETE FROM users WHERE pseudo = $1 RETURNING pseudo', [pseudo]);
166|             if (result.rows.length === 0) {
167|                 return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Utilisateur non trouvé' });
168|             }
169|             console.log(`🗑️ Utilisateur ${pseudo} supprimé de la base`);
170|             res.json({ success: true, message: 'Utilisateur supprimé' });
171|         } catch (err) {
172|             console.error('Erreur suppression utilisateur:', err.message);
173|             res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erreur serveur' });
174|         }
175|     });
176| 
177|     // ========== GET USER ==========
178|     app.post('/api/get-user', async (req, res) => {
179|         const { pseudo } = req.body;
180|         if (!pseudo) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Pseudo requis' });
181|         try {

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/modules/middleware/maintenance.js

1| ﻿// modules/middleware/maintenance.js
2| module.exports = function (pool) {
3|     return async (req, res, next) => {
4|         // Exclure assets
5|         if (req.path.match(/\.(css|js|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|json|webmanifest)$/i) ||
6|             req.path === '/api/admin/login' ||
7|             req.path === '/api/admin/maintenance' ||

16|         try {

18|             maintenance = result.rows[0]?.value === 'true';
19|         } catch (err) {
20|             console.error('Erreur maintenance:', err.message);
21|         }
22| 
23|         if (!maintenance) {
24|             return next();
25|         }

27|         if (isAdmin) {
28|             console.log(`👑 Admin ${req.session.adminUsername} accède à ${req.path}`);
29|             return next();
30|         }
31| 
32|         if (req.path !== '/') {
33|             console.log(`🚧 Redirection de ${req.path} vers /`);
34|             return res.redirect('/');
35|         }
36| 
37|         // Si on est à la racine, on continue vers la route /
38|         return next();
39|     };
40| };

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/sw.js

1| const CACHE_NAME = 'meetgay-v2';  // ← change la version pour forcer la mise à jour
2| const urlsToCache = [
3|     // '/', ← SUPPRIME (plus mis en cache)
4|     '/chat.html',
5|     '/manifest.json'
6| ];
7| 
8| // Installation
9| self.addEventListener('install', event => {
10|     event.waitUntil(
11|         caches.open(CACHE_NAME)
12|             .then(cache => cache.addAll(urlsToCache))
13|     );
14|     self.skipWaiting();  // ← force l'activation immédiate
15| });
16| 
17| // Récupération : PAS de cache pour '/' (il ira chercher sur le serveur)
18| self.addEventListener('fetch', event => {
19|     // Si la requête est pour la racine, on ne cache pas
20|     if (event.request.url === '/' || event.request.url.endsWith('/')) {
21|         event.respondWith(fetch(event.request));
22|         return;
23|     }
24| 
25|     event.respondWith(
26|         caches.match(event.request)
27|             .then(response => response || fetch(event.request))
28|     );
29| });
30| 
31| // Nettoyage des anciens caches
32| self.addEventListener('activate', event => {
33|     event.waitUntil(
34|         caches.keys().then(cacheNames => {
35|             return Promise.all(
36|                 cacheNames.map(name => {
37|                     if (name !== CACHE_NAME) {
38|                         return caches.delete(name);
39|                     }
40|                 })
41|             );
42|         })
43|     );
44|     self.clients.claim();  // ← prend le contrôle immédiatement
45| });

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/fp-bundle.js

1| (() => {
2|   // node_modules/@fingerprintjs/fingerprintjs/dist/fp.esm.js
3|   var version = "5.2.0";
4|   function wait(durationMs, resolveWith) {
5|     return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, durationMs, resolveWith));
6|   }
7|   function releaseEventLoop() {
8|     return new Promise((resolve) => {
9|       const channel = new MessageChannel();
10|       channel.port1.onmessage = () => resolve();
11|       channel.port2.postMessage(null);
12|     });
13|   }
14|   function requestIdleCallbackIfAvailable(fallbackTimeout, deadlineTimeout = Infinity) {
15|     const { requestIdleCallback } = window;
16|     if (requestIdleCallback) {
17|       return new Promise((resolve) => requestIdleCallback.call(window, () => resolve(), { timeout: deadlineTimeout }));
18|     } else {
19|       return wait(Math.min(fallbackTimeout, deadlineTimeout));
20|     }
21|   }
22|   function isPromise(value) {
23|     return !!value && typeof value.then === "function";
24|   }
25|   function awaitIfAsync(action, callback) {
26|     try {
27|       const returnedValue = action();
28|       if (isPromise(returnedValue)) {
29|         returnedValue.then((result) => callback(true, result), (error) => callback(false, error));
30|       } else {
31|         callback(true, returnedValue);
32|       }
33|     } catch (error) {
34|       callback(false, error);
35|     }
36|   }
37|   async function mapWithBreaks(items, callback, loopReleaseInterval = 16) {
38|     const results = Array(items.length);
39|     let lastLoopReleaseTime = Date.now();
40|     for (let i = 0; i < items.length; ++i) {
41|       results[i] = callback(items[i], i);
42|       const now = Date.now();
43|       if (now >= lastLoopReleaseTime + loopReleaseInterval) {
44|         lastLoopReleaseTime = now;
45|         await releaseEventLoop();
46|       }
47|     }
48|     return results;
49|   }
50|   function suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(promise) {
51|     promise.then(void 0, () => void 0);
52|     return promise;

54|   function includes(haystack, needle) {
55|     for (let i = 0, l = haystack.length; i < l; ++i) {
56|       if (haystack[i] === needle) {
57|         return true;
58|       }
59|     }
60|     return false;
61|   }
62|   function excludes(haystack, needle) {
63|     return !includes(haystack, needle);

77|   function round(value, base = 1) {
78|     if (Math.abs(base) >= 1) {
79|       return Math.round(value / base) * base;
80|     } else {
81|       const counterBase = 1 / base;
82|       return Math.round(value * counterBase) / counterBase;
83|     }
84|   }
85|   function parseSimpleCssSelector(selector) {
86|     var _a, _b;
87|     const errorMessage = `Unexpected syntax '${selector}'`;
88|     const tagMatch = /^\s*([a-z-]*)(.*)$/i.exec(selector);
89|     const tag = tagMatch[1] || void 0;
90|     const attributes = {};
91|     const partsRegex = /([.:#][\w-]+|\[.+?\])/gi;
92|     const addAttribute = (name, value) => {
93|       attributes[name] = attributes[name] || [];
94|       attributes[name].push(value);
95|     };
96|     for (; ; ) {
97|       const match = partsRegex.exec(tagMatch[2]);
98|       if (!match) {
99|         break;
100|       }
101|       const part = match[0];
102|       switch (part[0]) {
103|         case ".":
104|           addAttribute("class", part.slice(1));
105|           break;
106|         case "#":
107|           addAttribute("id", part.slice(1));
108|           break;
109|         case "[": {
110|           const attributeMatch = /^\[([\w-]+)([~|^$*]?=("(.*?)"|([\w-]+)))?(\s+[is])?\]$/.exec(part);
111|           if (attributeMatch) {
112|             addAttribute(attributeMatch[1], (_b = (_a = attributeMatch[4]) !== null && _a !== void 0 ? _a : attributeMatch[5]) !== null && _b !== void 0 ? _b : "");
113|           } else {
114|             throw new Error(errorMessage);
115|           }
116|           break;
117|         }
118|         default:
119|           throw new Error(errorMessage);
120|       }
121|     }
122|     return [tag, attributes];
123|   }
124|   function getUTF8Bytes(input) {
125|     const result = new Uint8Array(input.length);
126|     for (let i = 0; i < input.length; i++) {
127|       const charCode = input.charCodeAt(i);
128|       if (charCode > 127) {
129|         return new TextEncoder().encode(input);
130|       }
131|       result[i] = charCode;
132|     }
133|     return result;
134|   }
135|   function x64Add(m, n) {
136|     const m0 = m[0] >>> 16, m1 = m[0] & 65535, m2 = m[1] >>> 16, m3 = m[1] & 65535;
137|     const n0 = n[0] >>> 16, n1 = n[0] & 65535, n2 = n[1] >>> 16, n3 = n[1] & 65535;
138|     let o0 = 0, o1 = 0, o2 = 0, o3 = 0;
139|     o3 += m3 + n3;
140|     o2 += o3 >>> 16;
141|     o3 &= 65535;
142|     o2 += m2 + n2;
143|     o1 += o2 >>> 16;
144|     o2 &= 65535;
145|     o1 += m1 + n1;
146|     o0 += o1 >>> 16;
147|     o1 &= 65535;
148|     o0 += m0 + n0;
149|     o0 &= 65535;
150|     m[0] = o0 << 16 | o1;
151|     m[1] = o2 << 16 | o3;
152|   }
153|   function x64Multiply(m, n) {
154|     const m0 = m[0] >>> 16, m1 = m[0] & 65535, m2 = m[1] >>> 16, m3 = m[1] & 65535;
155|     const n0 = n[0] >>> 16, n1 = n[0] & 65535, n2 = n[1] >>> 16, n3 = n[1] & 65535;
156|     let o0 = 0, o1 = 0, o2 = 0, o3 = 0;
157|     o3 += m3 * n3;
158|     o2 += o3 >>> 16;
159|     o3 &= 65535;
160|     o2 += m2 * n3;
161|     o1 += o2 >>> 16;
162|     o2 &= 65535;
163|     o2 += m3 * n2;
164|     o1 += o2 >>> 16;
165|     o2 &= 65535;
166|     o1 += m1 * n3;
167|     o0 += o1 >>> 16;
168|     o1 &= 65535;
169|     o1 += m2 * n2;
170|     o0 += o1 >>> 16;
171|     o1 &= 65535;
172|     o1 += m3 * n1;
173|     o0 += o1 >>> 16;
174|     o1 &= 65535;
175|     o0 += m0 * n3 + m1 * n2 + m2 * n1 + m3 * n0;
176|     o0 &= 65535;
177|     m[0] = o0 << 16 | o1;
178|     m[1] = o2 << 16 | o3;
179|   }
180|   function x64Rotl(m, bits) {
181|     const m0 = m[0];
182|     bits %= 64;
183|     if (bits === 32) {
184|       m[0] = m[1];
185|       m[1] = m0;
186|     } else if (bits < 32) {
187|       m[0] = m0 << bits | m[1] >>> 32 - bits;
188|       m[1] = m[1] << bits | m0 >>> 32 - bits;
189|     } else {
190|       bits -= 32;
191|       m[0] = m[1] << bits | m0 >>> 32 - bits;
192|       m[1] = m0 << bits | m[1] >>> 32 - bits;
193|     }
194|   }
195|   function x64LeftShift(m, bits) {
196|     bits %= 64;
197|     if (bits === 0) {
198|       return;
199|     } else if (bits < 32) {
200|       m[0] = m[1] >>> 32 - bits;
201|       m[1] = m[1] << bits;
202|     } else {
203|       m[0] = m[1] << bits - 32;
204|       m[1] = 0;
205|     }
206|   }
207|   function x64Xor(m, n) {
208|     m[0] ^= n[0];
209|     m[1] ^= n[1];
210|   }
211|   var F1 = [4283543511, 3981806797];
212|   var F2 = [3301882366, 444984403];
213|   function x64Fmix(h) {
214|     const shifted = [0, h[0] >>> 1];
215|     x64Xor(h, shifted);
216|     x64Multiply(h, F1);
217|     shifted[1] = h[0] >>> 1;
218|     x64Xor(h, shifted);
219|     x64Multiply(h, F2);
220|     shifted[1] = h[0] >>> 1;
221|     x64Xor(h, shifted);
222|   }

228|   function x64hash128(input, seed) {
229|     const key = getUTF8Bytes(input);
230|     seed = seed || 0;
231|     const length = [0, key.length];
232|     const remainder = length[1] % 16;
233|     const bytes = length[1] - remainder;
234|     const h1 = [0, seed];
235|     const h2 = [0, seed];
236|     const k1 = [0, 0];
237|     const k2 = [0, 0];
238|     let i;
239|     for (i = 0; i < bytes; i = i + 16) {
240|       k1[0] = key[i + 4] | key[i + 5] << 8 | key[i + 6] << 16 | key[i + 7] << 24;
241|       k1[1] = key[i] | key[i + 1] << 8 | key[i + 2] << 16 | key[i + 3] << 24;
242|       k2[0] = key[i + 12] | key[i + 13] << 8 | key[i + 14] << 16 | key[i + 15] << 24;
243|       k2[1] = key[i + 8] | key[i + 9] << 8 | key[i + 10] << 16 | key[i + 11] << 24;
244|       x64Multiply(k1, C1);
245|       x64Rotl(k1, 31);
246|       x64Multiply(k1, C2);
247|       x64Xor(h1, k1);
248|       x64Rotl(h1, 27);
249|       x64Add(h1, h2);
250|       x64Multiply(h1, M$1);
251|       x64Add(h1, N1);
252|       x64Multiply(k2, C2);
253|       x64Rotl(k2, 33);
254|       x64Multiply(k2, C1);
255|       x64Xor(h2, k2);
256|       x64Rotl(h2, 31);
257|       x64Add(h2, h1);
258|       x64Multiply(h2, M$1);
259|       x64Add(h2, N2);
260|     }
261|     k1[0] = 0;
262|     k1[1] = 0;
263|     k2[0] = 0;
264|     k2[1] = 0;
265|     const val = [0, 0];
266|     switch (remainder) {
267|       case 15:
268|         val[1] = key[i + 14];
269|         x64LeftShift(val, 48);
270|         x64Xor(k2, val);
271|       // fallthrough
272|       case 14:
273|         val[1] = key[i + 13];
274|         x64LeftShift(val, 40);
275|         x64Xor(k2, val);
276|       // fallthrough
277|       case 13:
278|         val[1] = key[i + 12];
279|         x64LeftShift(val, 32);
280|         x64Xor(k2, val);
281|       // fallthrough
282|       case 12:
283|         val[1] = key[i + 11];
284|         x64LeftShift(val, 24);
285|         x64Xor(k2, val);
286|       // fallthrough
287|       case 11:
288|         val[1] = key[i + 10];
289|         x64LeftShift(val, 16);
290|         x64Xor(k2, val);
291|       // fallthrough
292|       case 10:
293|         val[1] = key[i + 9];
294|         x64LeftShift(val, 8);
295|         x64Xor(k2, val);
296|       // fallthrough
297|       case 9:
298|         val[1] = key[i + 8];
299|         x64Xor(k2, val);
300|         x64Multiply(k2, C2);
301|         x64Rotl(k2, 33);
302|         x64Multiply(k2, C1);
303|         x64Xor(h2, k2);
304|       // fallthrough
305|       case 8:
306|         val[1] = key[i + 7];
307|         x64LeftShift(val, 56);
308|         x64Xor(k1, val);
309|       // fallthrough
310|       case 7:
311|         val[1] = key[i + 6];
312|         x64LeftShift(val, 48);
313|         x64Xor(k1, val);
314|       // fallthrough
315|       case 6:
316|         val[1] = key[i + 5];
317|         x64LeftShift(val, 40);
318|         x64Xor(k1, val);
319|       // fallthrough
320|       case 5:
321|         val[1] = key[i + 4];
322|         x64LeftShift(val, 32);
323|         x64Xor(k1, val);
324|       // fallthrough
325|       case 4:
326|         val[1] = key[i + 3];
327|         x64LeftShift(val, 24);
328|         x64Xor(k1, val);
329|       // fallthrough
330|       case 3:
331|         val[1] = key[i + 2];
332|         x64LeftShift(val, 16);
333|         x64Xor(k1, val);
334|       // fallthrough
335|       case 2:
336|         val[1] = key[i + 1];
337|         x64LeftShift(val, 8);
338|         x64Xor(k1, val);
339|       // fallthrough
340|       case 1:
341|         val[1] = key[i];
342|         x64Xor(k1, val);
343|         x64Multiply(k1, C1);
344|         x64Rotl(k1, 31);
345|         x64Multiply(k1, C2);
346|         x64Xor(h1, k1);
347|     }
348|     x64Xor(h1, length);
349|     x64Xor(h2, length);
350|     x64Add(h1, h2);
351|     x64Add(h2, h1);
352|     x64Fmix(h1);
353|     x64Fmix(h2);
354|     x64Add(h1, h2);
355|     x64Add(h2, h1);
356|     return ("00000000" + (h1[0] >>> 0).toString(16)).slice(-8) + ("00000000" + (h1[1] >>> 0).toString(16)).slice(-8) + ("00000000" + (h2[0] >>> 0).toString(16)).slice(-8) + ("00000000" + (h2[1] >>> 0).toString(16)).slice(-8);
357|   }

374|   function loadSource(source, sourceOptions) {
375|     const sourceLoadPromise = suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(new Promise((resolveLoad) => {
376|       const loadStartTime = Date.now();
377|       awaitIfAsync(source.bind(null, sourceOptions), (...loadArgs) => {
378|         const loadDuration = Date.now() - loadStartTime;
379|         if (!loadArgs[0]) {
380|           return resolveLoad(() => ({ error: loadArgs[1], duration: loadDuration }));
381|         }
382|         const loadResult = loadArgs[1];
383|         if (isFinalResultLoaded(loadResult)) {
384|           return resolveLoad(() => ({ value: loadResult, duration: loadDuration }));
385|         }
386|         resolveLoad(() => new Promise((resolveGet) => {
387|           const getStartTime = Date.now();
388|           awaitIfAsync(loadResult, (...getArgs) => {
389|             const duration = loadDuration + Date.now() - getStartTime;
390|             if (!getArgs[0]) {
391|               return resolveGet({ error: getArgs[1], duration });
392|             }
393|             resolveGet({ value: getArgs[1], duration });
394|           });
395|         }));
396|       });
397|     }));
398|     return function getComponent() {
399|       return sourceLoadPromise.then((finalizeSource) => finalizeSource());
400|     };
401|   }
402|   function loadSources(sources2, sourceOptions, excludeSources, loopReleaseInterval) {
403|     const includedSources = Object.keys(sources2).filter((sourceKey) => excludes(excludeSources, sourceKey));
404|     const sourceGettersPromise = suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(mapWithBreaks(includedSources, (sourceKey) => loadSource(sources2[sourceKey], sourceOptions), loopReleaseInterval));
405|     return async function getComponents() {
406|       const sourceGetters = await sourceGettersPromise;
407|       const componentPromises = await mapWithBreaks(sourceGetters, (sourceGetter) => suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(sourceGetter()), loopReleaseInterval);
408|       const componentArray = await Promise.all(componentPromises);
409|       const components = {};
410|       for (let index2 = 0; index2 < includedSources.length; ++index2) {
411|         components[includedSources[index2]] = componentArray[index2];
412|       }
413|       return components;
414|     };
415|   }

601|         // `typechange` is deprecated, but it's still present on Android (tested on Chrome Mobile 117)

603|         // Note: this expression returns true on ChromeOS, so additional detectors are required to avoid false-positives
604|         n[c] && "ontypechange" in n[c],
605|         !("sinkId" in new Audio())
606|       ]) >= 2;
607|     } else if (isItGecko) {
608|       return countTruthy(["onorientationchange" in w, "orientation" in w, /android/i.test(n.appVersion)]) >= 2;
609|     } else {
610|       return false;
611|     }
612|   }

633|   function getUnstableAudioFingerprint() {
634|     const w = window;
635|     const AudioContext2 = w.OfflineAudioContext || w.webkitOfflineAudioContext;
636|     if (!AudioContext2) {
637|       return -2;
638|     }
639|     if (doesBrowserSuspendAudioContext()) {
640|       return -1;
641|     }
642|     const hashFromIndex = 4500;
643|     const hashToIndex = 5e3;
644|     const context = new AudioContext2(1, hashToIndex, 44100);
645|     const oscillator = context.createOscillator();
646|     oscillator.type = "triangle";
647|     oscillator.frequency.value = 1e4;
648|     const compressor = context.createDynamicsCompressor();
649|     compressor.threshold.value = -50;
650|     compressor.knee.value = 40;
651|     compressor.ratio.value = 12;
652|     compressor.attack.value = 0;
653|     compressor.release.value = 0.25;
654|     oscillator.connect(compressor);
655|     compressor.connect(context.destination);
656|     oscillator.start(0);
657|     const [renderPromise, finishRendering] = startRenderingAudio(context);
658|     const fingerprintPromise = suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(renderPromise.then((buffer) => getHash(buffer.getChannelData(0).subarray(hashFromIndex)), (error) => {
659|       if (error.name === "timeout" || error.name === "suspended") {
660|         return -3;
661|       }
662|       throw error;
663|     }));
664|     return () => {
665|       finishRendering();
666|       return fingerprintPromise;
667|     };
668|   }
669|   function doesBrowserSuspendAudioContext() {
670|     return isWebKit() && !isDesktopWebKit() && !isWebKit606OrNewer();
671|   }
672|   function doesBrowserPerformAntifingerprinting() {
673|     return (
674|       // Safari ≥17
675|       isWebKit() && isWebKit616OrNewer() && isSafariWebKit() || // Samsung Internet ≥26
676|       isChromium() && isSamsungInternet() && isChromium122OrNewer()
677|     );
678|   }
679|   function startRenderingAudio(context) {
680|     const renderTryMaxCount = 3;
681|     const renderRetryDelay = 500;
682|     const runningMaxAwaitTime = 500;
683|     const runningSufficientTime = 5e3;
684|     let finalize = () => void 0;
685|     const resultPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
686|       let isFinalized = false;
687|       let renderTryCount = 0;
688|       let startedRunningAt = 0;
689|       context.oncomplete = (event) => resolve(event.renderedBuffer);
690|       const startRunningTimeout = () => {
691|         setTimeout(() => reject(makeInnerError(
692|           "timeout"
693|           /* InnerErrorName.Timeout */
694|         )), Math.min(runningMaxAwaitTime, startedRunningAt + runningSufficientTime - Date.now()));
695|       };
696|       const tryRender = () => {
697|         try {
698|           const renderingPromise = context.startRendering();
699|           if (isPromise(renderingPromise)) {
700|             suppressUnhandledRejectionWarning(renderingPromise);
701|           }
702|           switch (context.state) {
703|             case "running":
704|               startedRunningAt = Date.now();
705|               if (isFinalized) {
706|                 startRunningTimeout();
707|               }
708|               break;
709|             // Sometimes the audio context doesn't start after calling `startRendering` (in addition to the cases where
710|             // audio context doesn't start at all). A known case is starting an audio context when the browser tab is in
711|             // background on iPhone. Retries usually help in this case.
712|             case "suspended":
713|               if (!document.hidden) {
714|                 renderTryCount++;
715|               }
716|               if (isFinalized && renderTryCount >= renderTryMaxCount) {
717|                 reject(makeInnerError(
718|                   "suspended"
719|                   /* InnerErrorName.Suspended */
720|                 ));
721|               } else {
722|                 setTimeout(tryRender, renderRetryDelay);
723|               }
724|               break;
725|           }
726|         } catch (error) {
727|           reject(error);
728|         }
729|       };
730|       tryRender();
731|       finalize = () => {
732|         if (!isFinalized) {
733|           isFinalized = true;
734|           if (startedRunningAt > 0) {
735|             startRunningTimeout();
736|           }
737|         }
738|       };
739|     });
740|     return [resultPromise, finalize];
741|   }
742|   function getHash(signal) {
743|     let hash = 0;
744|     for (let i = 0; i < signal.length; ++i) {
745|       hash += Math.abs(signal[i]);
746|     }
747|     return hash;
748|   }

807|   function selectorToElement(selector) {
808|     const [tag, attributes] = parseSimpleCssSelector(selector);
809|     const element = document.createElement(tag !== null && tag !== void 0 ? tag : "div");
810|     for (const name of Object.keys(attributes)) {
811|       const value = attributes[name].join(" ");
812|       if (name === "style") {
813|         addStyleString(element.style, value);
814|       } else {
815|         element.setAttribute(name, value);
816|       }
817|     }
818|     return element;
819|   }
820|   function addStyleString(style, source) {
821|     for (const property of source.split(";")) {
822|       const match = /^\s*([\w-]+)\s*:\s*(.+?)(\s*!([\w-]+))?\s*$/.exec(property);
823|       if (match) {
824|         const [, name, value, , priority] = match;
825|         style.setProperty(name, value, priority || "");
826|       }
827|     }
828|   }
829|   function isAnyParentCrossOrigin() {
830|     let currentWindow = window;
831|     for (; ; ) {
832|       const parentWindow = currentWindow.parent;
833|       if (!parentWindow || parentWindow === currentWindow) {
834|         return false;
835|       }
836|       try {
837|         if (parentWindow.location.origin !== currentWindow.location.origin) {
838|           return true;
839|         }
840|       } catch (error) {
841|         if (error instanceof Error && error.name === "SecurityError") {
842|           return true;
843|         }
844|         throw error;
845|       }
846|       currentWindow = parentWindow;
847|     }
848|   }

952|   function getPlugins() {

956|     }
957|     const plugins = [];

1215|       const timezone = new DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone;
1216|       if (timezone) {
1217|         return timezone;
1218|       }
1219|     }
1220|     const offset = -getTimezoneOffset();
1221|     return `UTC${offset >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${offset}`;
1222|   }
1223|   function getTimezoneOffset() {
1224|     const currentYear = (/* @__PURE__ */ new Date()).getFullYear();
1225|     return Math.max(
1226|       // `getTimezoneOffset` returns a number as a string in some unidentified cases
1227|       toFloat(new Date(currentYear, 0, 1).getTimezoneOffset()),
1228|       toFloat(new Date(currentYear, 6, 1).getTimezoneOffset())
1229|     );
1230|   }
1231|   function getSessionStorage() {
1232|     try {
1233|       return !!window.sessionStorage;
1234|     } catch (error) {
1235|       return true;
1236|     }
1237|   }

1261|   function getPlatform() {
1262|     const { platform } = navigator;
1263|     if (platform === "MacIntel") {
1264|       if (isWebKit() && !isDesktopWebKit()) {
1265|         return isIPad() ? "iPad" : "iPhone";
1266|       }
1267|     }
1268|     return platform;
1269|   }

1272|   }
1273|   function getVendorFlavors() {
1274|     const flavors = [];
1275|     for (const key of [
1276|       // Blink and some browsers on iOS
1277|       "chrome",
1278|       // Safari on macOS
1279|       "safari",
1280|       // Chrome on iOS (checked in 85 on 13 and 87 on 14)
1281|       "__crWeb",
1282|       "__gCrWeb",
1283|       // Yandex Browser on iOS, macOS and Android (checked in 21.2 on iOS 14, macOS and Android)
1284|       "yandex",
1285|       // Yandex Browser on iOS (checked in 21.2 on 14)
1286|       "__yb",
1287|       "__ybro",
1288|       // Firefox on iOS (checked in 32 on 14)
1289|       "__firefox__",
1290|       // Edge on iOS (checked in 46 on 14)
1291|       "__edgeTrackingPreventionStatistics",
1292|       "webkit",
1293|       // Opera Touch on iOS (checked in 2.6 on 14)
1294|       "oprt",
1295|       // Samsung Internet on Android (checked in 11.1)
1296|       "samsungAr",
1297|       // UC Browser on Android (checked in 12.10 and 13.0)
1298|       "ucweb",
1299|       "UCShellJava",
1300|       // Puffin on Android (checked in 9.0)
1301|       "puffinDevice"
1302|       // UC on iOS and Opera on Android have no specific global variables
1303|       // Edge for Android isn't checked
1304|     ]) {
1305|       const value = window[key];
1306|       if (value && typeof value === "object") {
1307|         flavors.push(key);
1308|       }
1309|     }
1310|     return flavors.sort();
1311|   }

1318|       return result;
1319|     } catch (e) {
1320|       return false;
1321|     }
1322|   }

1586|   async function getDomBlockers({ debug } = {}) {
1587|     if (!isApplicable()) {
1588|       return void 0;
1589|     }
1590|     const filters = getFilters();
1591|     const filterNames = Object.keys(filters);
1592|     const allSelectors = [].concat(...filterNames.map((filterName) => filters[filterName]));
1593|     const blockedSelectors = await getBlockedSelectors(allSelectors);
1594|     if (debug) {
1595|       printDebug(filters, blockedSelectors);
1596|     }
1597|     const activeBlockers = filterNames.filter((filterName) => {
1598|       const selectors = filters[filterName];
1599|       const blockedCount = countTruthy(selectors.map((selector) => blockedSelectors[selector]));
1600|       return blockedCount > selectors.length * 0.6;
1601|     });
1602|     activeBlockers.sort();
1603|     return activeBlockers;
1604|   }
1605|   function isApplicable() {
1606|     return isWebKit() || isAndroid();
1607|   }
1608|   async function getBlockedSelectors(selectors) {
1609|     var _a;
1610|     const d = document;
1611|     const root = d.createElement("div");
1612|     const elements = new Array(selectors.length);
1613|     const blockedSelectors = {};
1614|     forceShow(root);
1615|     for (let i = 0; i < selectors.length; ++i) {
1616|       const element = selectorToElement(selectors[i]);
1617|       if (element.tagName === "DIALOG") {
1618|         element.show();
1619|       }
1620|       const holder = d.createElement("div");
1621|       forceShow(holder);
1622|       holder.appendChild(element);
1623|       root.appendChild(holder);
1624|       elements[i] = element;
1625|     }
1626|     while (!d.body) {
1627|       await wait(50);
1628|     }
1629|     d.body.appendChild(root);
1630|     try {
1631|       for (let i = 0; i < selectors.length; ++i) {
1632|         if (!elements[i].offsetParent) {
1633|           blockedSelectors[selectors[i]] = true;
1634|         }
1635|       }

2248|     // Some sources can affect other sources (e.g. WebGL can affect canvas), so it's important to run these sources
2249|     // after other sources.
2250|     webGlBasics: getWebGlBasics,
2251|     webGlExtensions: getWebGlExtensions
2252|   };
2253|   function loadBuiltinSources(options) {
2254|     return loadSources(sources, options, []);
2255|   }
2256|   var commentTemplate = "$ if upgrade to Pro: https://fingerprint.com/github/?utm_source=oss&utm_medium=referral&utm_campaign=confidence_score";
2257|   function getConfidence(components) {
2258|     const openConfidenceScore = getOpenConfidenceScore(components);
2259|     const proConfidenceScore = deriveProConfidenceScore(openConfidenceScore);
2260|     return { score: openConfidenceScore, comment: commentTemplate.replace(/\$/g, `${proConfidenceScore}`) };
2261|   }
2262|   function getOpenConfidenceScore(components) {
2263|     if (isAndroid()) {
2264|       return 0.4;
2265|     }
2266|     if (isWebKit()) {
2267|       return isDesktopWebKit() && !(isWebKit616OrNewer() && isSafariWebKit()) ? 0.5 : 0.3;
2268|     }
2269|     const platform = "value" in components.platform ? components.platform.value : "";
2270|     if (/^Win/.test(platform)) {
2271|       return 0.6;
2272|     }
2273|     if (/^Mac/.test(platform)) {
2274|       return 0.5;
2275|     }
2276|     return 0.7;
2277|   }
2278|   function deriveProConfidenceScore(openConfidenceScore) {
2279|     return round(0.99 + 0.01 * openConfidenceScore, 1e-4);
2280|   }
2281|   function componentsToCanonicalString(components) {
2282|     let result = "";
2283|     for (const componentKey of Object.keys(components).sort()) {
2284|       const component = components[componentKey];
2285|       const value = "error" in component ? "error" : JSON.stringify(component.value);
2286|       result += `${result ? "|" : ""}${componentKey.replace(/([:|\\])/g, "\\$1")}:${value}`;
2287|     }
2288|     return result;
2289|   }
2290|   function componentsToDebugString(components) {
2291|     return JSON.stringify(components, (_key, value) => {
2292|       if (value instanceof Error) {
2293|         return errorToObject(value);
2294|       }
2295|       return value;
2296|     }, 2);
2297|   }
2298|   function hashComponents(components) {
2299|     return x64hash128(componentsToCanonicalString(components));
2300|   }
2301|   function makeLazyGetResult(components) {
2302|     let visitorIdCache;
2303|     const confidence = getConfidence(components);
2304|     return {
2305|       get visitorId() {
2306|         if (visitorIdCache === void 0) {
2307|           visitorIdCache = hashComponents(this.components);
2308|         }
2309|         return visitorIdCache;
2310|       },
2311|       set visitorId(visitorId) {
2312|         visitorIdCache = visitorId;
2313|       },
2314|       confidence,
2315|       components,
2316|       version
2317|     };
2318|   }
2319|   function prepareForSources(delayFallback = 50) {
2320|     return requestIdleCallbackIfAvailable(delayFallback, delayFallback * 2);
2321|   }
2322|   function makeAgent(getComponents, debug) {
2323|     const creationTime = Date.now();
2324|     return {
2325|       async get(options) {
2326|         const startTime = Date.now();
2327|         const components = await getComponents();
2328|         const result = makeLazyGetResult(components);
2329|         if (debug || (options === null || options === void 0 ? void 0 : options.debug)) {
2330|           console.log(`Copy the text below to get the debug data:
2331| 
2332| \`\`\`
2333| version: ${result.version}
2334| userAgent: ${navigator.userAgent}
2335| timeBetweenLoadAndGet: ${startTime - creationTime}
2336| visitorId: ${result.visitorId}
2337| components: ${componentsToDebugString(components)}
2338| \`\`\``);
2339|         }
2340|         return result;
2341|       }
2342|     };
2343|   }
2344|   function monitor() {
2345|     if (window.__fpjs_d_m || Math.random() >= 1e-3) {
2346|       return;
2347|     }
2348|     try {
2349|       const request = new XMLHttpRequest();
2350|       request.open("get", `https://m1.openfpcdn.io/fingerprintjs/v${version}/npm-monitoring`, true);
2351|       request.send();
2352|     } catch (error) {
2353|       console.error(error);
2354|     }
2355|   }
2356|   async function load(options = {}) {
2357|     const { delayFallback, debug, monitoring = true } = options;
2358|     if (monitoring) {
2359|       monitor();
2360|     }
2361|     await prepareForSources(delayFallback);
2362|     const getComponents = loadBuiltinSources({ cache: {}, debug });
2363|     return makeAgent(getComponents, debug);
2364|   }
2365|   var index = { load, hashComponents, componentsToDebugString };
2366| 
2367|   // public/js/fingerprint-source.js
2368|   (async () => {
2369|     try {
2370|       const fp = await index.load();
2371|       const result = await fp.get();
2372|       const visitorId = result.visitorId;
2373|       sessionStorage.setItem("fingerprint", visitorId);
2374|       window.currentFingerprint = visitorId;
2375|       console.log("\u{1F512} Fingerprint g\xE9n\xE9r\xE9:", visitorId);
2376|     } catch (err) {
2377|       console.error("\u274C Erreur fingerprint:", err);
2378|       const fallback = "temp_" + Date.now();
2379|       sessionStorage.setItem("fingerprint", fallback);
2380|       window.currentFingerprint = fallback;
2381|     }
2382|   })();
2383| })();

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/history.js

1| // history.js - Gestion de l'historique des conversations (bilingue)
2| 
3| let conversationHistory = {};
4| 
5| function addToHistory(contactPseudo, text, type, fromPseudo, toPseudo) {
6|     if (!conversationHistory[contactPseudo]) {
7|         conversationHistory[contactPseudo] = [];
8|     }
9|     conversationHistory[contactPseudo].push({
10|         text: text,
11|         type: type,
12|         from: fromPseudo,
13|         to: toPseudo,
14|         timestamp: new Date()
15|     });
16|     updateHistoryDisplay();
17| }
18| 
19| function updateHistoryDisplay() {
20|     const historyDiv = document.getElementById('historyList');
21|     const t = window.chatT || { noConversation: "Aucune conversation" };
22|     if (!historyDiv) return;
23| 
24|     const contacts = Object.keys(conversationHistory);
25| 
26|     if (contacts.length === 0) {
27|         historyDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-message" style="padding: 20px;">${t.noConversation}</div>`;
28|         return;
29|     }
30| 
31|     contacts.sort((a, b) => {
32|         const lastA = conversationHistory[a][conversationHistory[a].length - 1]?.timestamp || 0;
33|         const lastB = conversationHistory[b][conversationHistory[b].length - 1]?.timestamp || 0;
34|         return lastB - lastA;
35|     });
36| 
37|     historyDiv.innerHTML = '';
38| 
39|     contacts.forEach(contact => {
40|         const messages = conversationHistory[contact];
41|         if (!messages || messages.length === 0) return;
42| 
43|         const accordion = document.createElement('div');
44|         accordion.className = 'contact-accordion';
45| 
46|         const header = document.createElement('div');
47|         header.className = 'contact-header';
48|         header.innerHTML = `<span>💬 ${escapeHtml(contact)}</span><span class="badge">${messages.length}</span>`;
49| 
50|         const messagesDiv = document.createElement('div');
51|         messagesDiv.className = 'contact-messages';
52| 
53|         messages.forEach(msg => {
54|             const msgDiv = document.createElement('div');
55|             msgDiv.className = `history-message ${msg.type}`;
56|             const sender = msg.type === 'sent' ? `📤 Moi → ${escapeHtml(contact)}` : `✉️ ${escapeHtml(msg.from)}`;
57|             const timeStr = formatTime(msg.timestamp);
58|             msgDiv.innerHTML = `
59|                 <div class="message-sender">${sender}</div>
60|                 <div class="message-text">${escapeHtml(msg.text)}</div>
61|                 <div class="message-time">${timeStr}</div>
62|             `;
63|             messagesDiv.appendChild(msgDiv);
64|         });
65| 
66|         header.onclick = () => messagesDiv.classList.toggle('open');
67|         accordion.appendChild(header);
68|         accordion.appendChild(messagesDiv);
69|         historyDiv.appendChild(accordion);
70|     });
71| }

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/admin.js

1| // ============================================================
2| // admin.js - Panel Admin (version base de données)
3| // ============================================================
4| 
5| // Variables globales
6| let allUsers = [];
7| let filteredUsers = [];
8| 
9| // Éléments DOM
10| const usersListDiv = document.getElementById('usersList');
11| const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
12| const roleFilter = document.getElementById('roleFilter');
13| const statusFilter = document.getElementById('statusFilter');
14| const searchBtn = document.getElementById('searchBtn');
15| const maintenanceBtn = document.getElementById('maintenanceBtn');
16| const backupDbBtn = document.getElementById('backupDbBtn');
17| const cleanupBtn = document.getElementById('cleanupBtn');

19| // ========== 1. CHARGEMENT DES UTILISATEURS ==========
20| async function loadUsers() {
21|     try {
22|         const response = await fetch('/api/admin/users');
23| 
24|         if (!response.ok) {
25|             usersListDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">❌ Erreur chargement utilisateurs</div>';
26|             return;
27|         }
28| 
29|         allUsers = await response.json();
30|         filteredUsers = [...allUsers];
31| 
32|         updateStats();
33|         renderUsersTable();
34| 
35|     } catch (err) {
36|         console.error('Erreur loadUsers:', err);
37|         usersListDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">❌ Erreur serveur</div>';
38|     }
39| }
40| 
41| // ========== 2. METTRE À JOUR LES STATS ==========
42| function updateStats() {
43|     const totalUsers = allUsers.length;
44|     const totalWarns = allUsers.reduce((sum, u) => sum + (u.warnings || 0), 0);
45|     const totalBanned = allUsers.filter(u => u.is_banned).length;
46|     const totalModos = allUsers.filter(u => u.role === 'modo' || u.role === 'admin').length;
47| 
48|     document.getElementById('totalUsers').innerText = totalUsers;
49|     document.getElementById('totalWarns').innerText = totalWarns;
50|     document.getElementById('totalBanned').innerText = totalBanned;
51|     document.getElementById('totalModos').innerText = totalModos;
52| }
53| 
54| // ========== 3. AFFICHER LE TABLEAU DES UTILISATEURS ==========
55| function renderUsersTable() {
56|     if (filteredUsers.length === 0) {
57|         usersListDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">👀 Aucun utilisateur trouvé</div>';
58|         return;
59|     }
60| 
61|     let html = `
62|         <table>
63|             <thead>
64|                 <tr>
65|                     <th>Pseudo</th>
66|                     <th>Âge</th>
67|                     <th>Rôle</th>
68|                     <th>⚠️ Warns</th>
69|                     <th>Statut</th>
70|                     <th>Actions</th>
71|                 </tr>
72|             </thead>
73|             <tbody>
74|     `;
75| 
76|     filteredUsers.forEach(u => {
77|         let statusBadge = '';
78|         let statusText = '';
79|         if (u.is_banned) {
80|             statusBadge = 'status-banned';
81|             statusText = '🚫 Banni';
82|         } else if ((u.warnings || 0) >= 3) {
83|             statusBadge = 'status-warned';
84|             statusText = '⚠️ Averti';
85|         } else {
86|             statusBadge = 'status-active';
87|             statusText = '✅ Actif';
88|         }
89| 
90|         let roleDisplay = u.role || 'visiteur';
91|         if (roleDisplay === 'admin') roleDisplay = '👑 Admin';
92|         else if (roleDisplay === 'modo') roleDisplay = '👮 Modo';
93|         else if (roleDisplay === 'user') roleDisplay = '👤 Membre';
94|         else roleDisplay = '👥 Visiteur';
95| 
96|         html += `
97|             <tr data-pseudo="${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}">
98|                 <td><strong>${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}</strong></td>
99|                 <td>${u.age || '?'}</td>
100|                 <td>${roleDisplay}</td>
101|                 <td>${u.warnings || 0}</td>
102|                 <td><span class="status-badge ${statusBadge}">${statusText}</span></td>
103|                 <td class="action-buttons">
104|         `;
105| 
106|         if (!u.is_banned) {
107|             html += `<button class="action-btn btn-warn" onclick="warnUser('${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}')">⚠️ Warn</button>`;
108|             html += `<button class="action-btn btn-ban" onclick="banUser('${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}')">🚫 Ban</button>`;
109|         } else {
110|             html += `<button class="action-btn btn-unban" onclick="unbanUser('${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}')">🔓 Unban</button>`;
111|         }
112| 
113|         if (u.role !== 'admin' && u.role !== 'modo') {
114|             html += `<button class="action-btn btn-modo" onclick="setModo('${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}')">👮 Modo</button>`;
115|         }
116| 
117|         if (u.role === 'modo') {
118|             html += `<button class="action-btn btn-admin" onclick="setAdmin('${escapeHtml(u.pseudo)}')">👑 Admin</button>`;
119|         }
120| 
121|         html += `</td></tr>`;
122|     });
123| 
124|     html += `</tbody></table>`;
125|     usersListDiv.innerHTML = html;
126| }
127| 
128| // ========== 4. FILTRES ET RECHERCHE ==========
129| function applyFilters() {
130|     const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();
131|     const role = roleFilter.value;
132|     const status = statusFilter.value;
133| 
134|     filteredUsers = allUsers.filter(u => {
135|         if (searchTerm && !u.pseudo.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) return false;
136| 
137|         if (role !== 'all') {
138|             if (role === 'admin' && u.role !== 'admin') return false;
139|             if (role === 'modo' && u.role !== 'modo') return false;
140|             if (role === 'user' && u.role !== 'user') return false;
141|             if (role === 'guest' && (u.role && u.role !== 'guest')) return false;
142|         }
143| 
144|         if (status !== 'all') {
145|             if (status === 'banned' && !u.is_banned) return false;
146|             if (status === 'warned' && (!u.warnings || u.warnings < 3)) return false;
147|             if (status === 'active' && (u.is_banned || (u.warnings || 0) >= 3)) return false;
148|         }
149| 
150|         return true;
151|     });
152| 
153|     renderUsersTable();
154| }
155| 
156| // ========== 5. ACTIONS ADMIN ==========
157| async function warnUser(pseudo) {
158|     if (typeof MGPopup !== 'undefined') {
159|         MGPopup.show({
160|             title: '⚠️ Confirmation',
161|             message: `Envoyer un avertissement à ${pseudo} ?`,
162|             onConfirm: async () => {
163|                 try {
164|                     const response = await fetch('/api/admin/warn', {
165|                         method: 'POST',
166|                         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
167|                         body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo })
168|                     });
169| 
170|                     if (response.ok) {
171|                         MGPopup.show({
172|                             title: '✅ Succès',
173|                             message: `${pseudo} a reçu un avertissement.`,
174|                             onConfirm: () => loadUsers()
175|                         });
176|                     } else {
177|                         MGPopup.show({
178|                             title: '❌ Erreur',
179|                             message: 'Erreur lors de l\'envoi de l\'avertissement.',
180|                             onConfirm: () => { }
181|                         });
182|                     }
183|                 } catch (err) {
184|                     console.error(err);
185|                     MGPopup.show({
186|                         title: '❌ Erreur réseau',
187|                         message: 'Impossible de contacter le serveur.',
188|                         onConfirm: () => { }
189|                     });
190|                 }
191|             },
192|             onCancel: () => { }
193|         });
194|     } else {
195|         // Fallback
196|         if (!confirm(`⚠️ Envoyer un avertissement à ${pseudo} ?`)) return;
197|         try {
198|             const response = await fetch('/api/admin/warn', {
199|                 method: 'POST',
200|                 headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
201|                 body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo })
202|             });
203|             if (response.ok) {
204|                 alert(`✅ ${pseudo} a reçu un avertissement`);
205|                 await loadUsers();
206|             } else {
207|                 alert('❌ Erreur');
208|             }
209|         } catch (err) {
210|             console.error(err);
211|             alert('❌ Erreur réseau');
212|         }
213|     }
214| }

246|                         });
247|                     }

250|                     MGPopup.show({

253|                         onConfirm: () => { }
254|                     });
255|                 }
256|             },
257|             onCancel: () => { }
